Current Affairs Commentary

The Competition Between the Naval and Air Forces of Japan and the United States - The Situation in the Pacific After the Failure of the Disarmament Conference -

The relationship between Japan and the United States has recently shown a trend of easing due to intensified economic conflicts between Britain and Japan, and tense diplomatic relations between Japan and the Soviet Union. Japan interprets this easing as stemming from the fact that there are few active conflicts in the economic realm between Japan and the United States and ample room for harmonization, with the exchange of cotton and raw silk being a historical source. The severity of the global economic panic has made such mutual needs even more critical. As for the United States, it is busy stabilizing its domestic economic panic and urgently seeking to open up overseas markets through peaceful means. It cannot but temporarily remain silent regarding Japan's military adventurous actions. However, can the aforementioned interests between Japan and the United States truly be harmonized, and will the deterioration of political relations not be severe? Everyone knows this is not the case. It is evidently a diplomatic maneuver by the Japanese to stabilize the morale of their people amidst their surrounded situation, hoping to reduce the obstacles they face internationally.

Originally, Japan's rise in the Pacific was greatly aided by Britain. Before the Russo-Japanese War, the power of Imperial Russia expanded, seeking to extend its reach into the Pacific to encompass China and dominate the seas, while also crossing the Huihui ethnic groups from Central Asia to peer into India. To protect its Eastern markets and the security of its rule over India, Britain had to prevent the excessive expansion of Imperial Russia's power. Consequently, it had no choice but to support Japan and suppress Russia. However, since the Russian Revolution, the fundamental national policy of Russia has changed. Although Britain cannot be entirely without vigilance towards it, Japan's rapid advance is even more pronounced than that of Russia in the past. The expansion of its economic power and the swelling of its naval strength have caused Britain to feel deeply uneasy in the Far Eastern markets. Therefore, Britain had to first secure its frontiers, making the area west of Hong Kong its sphere of maritime influence, with the Far Eastern markets as its vanguard and India as its base. The export of Japanese goods to India is subject to certain restrictions. Consequently, the relationship between Britain and Japan has shifted from alliance to separation and has become adversarial.

Japan and the Soviet Union have historically had many rifts, and their theoretical standpoints are also entirely incompatible. However, there is still room for maneuver in international relations. However, after Japan provoked the September 18th Incident, its relations with the Soviet Union have worsened. The infringement of the Soviet Union's acquired rights in northern Manchuria is not limited to the Chinese Eastern Railway alone. Vladivostok is at risk of being invaded, and Baikal cannot avoid being controlled from the flanks. At the same time, Japan is also the continental military power in East Asia, and its traditional hypothetical enemy is the Soviet Union. The differences between the two countries in political and economic standpoints have evolved into serious military preparedness. Given an opportunity, there is the potential for explosion.

Amidst the exposure of this crisis, the relationship between Japan and the United States is merely a shift in a portion of public opinion, while the United States and the Soviet Union are accelerating the restoration of diplomatic relations. Although the restoration focuses on economics, it will also have a significant impact politically, especially on the current situation in the Far East. Therefore, Japan has repeatedly changed its second supplementary naval shipbuilding plan to construct two aircraft carriers, two cruisers, and destroyers and submarines within the limits of the London Treaty, with a total of 23 vessels to be built. In addition, there are 26 transport ships and repair ships outside the limits. The air force has also suddenly increased by eight squadrons. Although its naval shipbuilding budget has been reduced to 450 million Japanese yen, it still retains the addition of future budgets. Can such a large-scale expansion of warships fail to alarm the United States and alert Britain?

The forward military bases of the United States in the Far East are Guam and Manila. The naval base of the United States on the Pacific coast is more than 2,000 nautical miles from Pearl Harbor in Hawaii. Pearl Harbor is more than 3,300 nautical miles from Guam. Manila is also over 1,500 nautical miles from Guam. Even connecting the Aleutian Islands with the naval port near Bremerton-Seattle is not easy. Japan's forward base, Penghu Island in the Taiwan Strait, is only 600 miles from Manila and only 1,500 nautical miles from Japan itself. Therefore, Japan's defense is very easy, and it is not too difficult to advance on Guam and peer into the Philippines. Moreover, the sea route from Okinawa to Guam is only 850 nautical miles. Japan's forward naval base in the Pacific, Ogasawara Island, is only 550 nautical miles from Yokosuka. Its operations are flexible, and its actions are swift, far beyond what the United States can achieve. Recently, it has also been working hard to expand its naval air force. Although its military strength is not as great as that of the United States, it has more than enough for defense, and it is not difficult to invade American territories. Furthermore, with the rapid movement and violent explosive power of the air force, the ability of the United States to defend the Philippines is ultimately difficult to ensure stability. Given the immense threat felt towards the development of Far Eastern markets, the competition between the naval and air forces of Japan and the United States will become turbulent waves in the Pacific in the future, and will not stop until it triggers a final war.

Roman Talks Conclude, Russian Foreign Minister Issues Declaration, Reiterating Desire to Maintain Peace, Denouncing Disarmament Conference as a Mere Corpse, Remaining Silent on Far East Discussions, Not Discussing Reform of the League of Nations, Religious Policy Unchanged, Litvinov Leaves Rome for Berlin Last Night, Denying Possibility of Russo-German Non-Aggression Pact

Rome - Today, Soviet Russian Foreign Minister Litvinov issued a lengthy statement to the press, strongly asserting Russia's desire to maintain peace with its neighbors, and stating that in the past ten years, there has never been a discussion of friendly relations between Italy and Russia like today's. The recognition of Soviet Russia by the United States has not changed the existing relations between Italy and Russia. This afternoon, Litvinov attended a farewell banquet hosted by American Ambassador Lang, accompanied by key members of the American and Russian embassies. In the evening, Mr. Litvinov attended a farewell banquet hosted by the Turkish ambassador. At 9:30 tonight, the Soviet Russian Foreign Minister will depart for Berlin to meet with the first American Ambassador to Russia, Bullitt, there. (5th National Telegram)

Rome - Russian Foreign Minister Litvinov told guests today, regarding the results of his trip, that he had frank talks with American President Roosevelt, Italian leader Mussolini, French Foreign Minister Poncet, and German Foreign Minister Neurath. Before returning to Russia, he will see the German Foreign Minister again. He denounced the disarmament conference as a corpse, which is entirely reasonable, as some countries are preparing for war. To speak of disarmament at this time is simply a waste of time. As for the reorganization of the League of Nations and the issue of Soviet Russia joining the League of Nations, it has not been discussed. He also had no contact with the Roman Catholic Church, as Soviet Russia's religious policy has not changed. Russia still prohibits religious propaganda. Litvinov acknowledged that he had discussed the Far East issue but did not wish to elaborate. He also denied the possibility of a Russo-German non-aggression treaty. (5th Reuters Dispatch)

Emphasis on Enhancing German-Russian Relations

Rome - Tonight, Prime Minister Mussolini will attend a banquet at the Russian embassy, where both sides will continue negotiations. It is now widely rumored that the Russian Foreign Minister has met with the German Ambassador, but this claim is difficult to prove. Assuming it did happen, the meeting must have been extremely secret. (4th Reuters Dispatch)

(London) - British newspaper reporters reported on Russian Commissioner Litvinov's trip to Italy, stating that Mr. Litvinov and Italian Prime Minister Mussolini's talks focused heavily on enhancing German-Russian relations. There is a possibility of Soviet Russia joining the Four-Power Pact. Daily Telegraph reporters also stated that they are now certain that the Italian Prime Minister aims to finalize a Russo-German non-aggression agreement. (4th National Telegram)

Rumors of a Trip to Vienna

Vienna - The "Neue Freie Presse" reports that, according to reliable sources, Soviet Foreign Minister Litvinov will come to Vienna from Rome tomorrow (Wednesday). (5th Havas Dispatch)

Russia and Italy Discuss Religious Issues, American Postmaster General Will Serve as Intermediary

Rome - Litvinov toured the suburbs today. American Postmaster General Farley, who came from New York, is still here engaging in diplomatic activities. Mr. Farley met with the Pope and his Secretary of State today, and will pay a visit to Italian Prime Minister Mussolini tomorrow. As one of the leaders of American Catholicism, he is here to explain the religious freedom issue for Americans in Russia under the Russo-American agreement. He will likely serve as an intermediary in negotiations between Litvinov, the Holy See, and the Italian government, as the Holy See cannot directly negotiate with the Russian Foreign Minister because Soviet Russia is an anti-Christian nation. If the Holy See can indirectly persuade Russia to allow people of all countries to enjoy religious freedom within Russia, the Holy See will recognize the Russian government. In this case, the relations between Soviet Russia and Catholic countries will become closer, especially with Poland. (4th Dentsu Telegram)

Italy Opposes German-Austrian Union

Vienna - Newspapers have much coverage of the Spanish election events and Litvinov's trip to Rome. News from Rome states that Italian authorities have declared that Italy will oppose the German-Austrian union in any case. The newspapers of Vienna do not criticize this news, as Italy's determination to maintain Austria's political independence is already known to the world and need not be elaborated upon. (4th Havas Dispatch)

Russian Deputy Foreign Minister Hosts Banquet for German Ambassador

(Moscow) - The Russian Deputy Foreign Minister hosted a banquet tonight to welcome the new German Ambassador, Nadolny. Mr. Nadolny said during the banquet that his main purpose is to make the relations between the two countries closer. He believes that his ability to act will be able to cope with the true spirit of cooperation between the two countries. (4th National Telegram)

Conflicting Impressions from Various Parties

Rome - The press is commenting on the communique released after the meeting between Litvinov and Mussolini, saying that although the detailed circumstances of the talks are unknown, the two men seem to have discussed disarmament, the Danube River issue, and the Far East issue, and intend to consider them outside the League of Nations, using methods that all other powers can recognize. One phrase in the communique has been emphasized by various newspapers, namely, "Litvinov and Mussolini believe that the general political situation can be improved in accordance with the spirit of the Treaty of Friendship between Italy and Soviet Russia." "La Stampa" stated that there are several major issues to be resolved outside the League of Nations, such as the relations between Soviet Russia, Germany, and Japan, which are unrelated to Geneva because the three countries are not members of the League of Nations. "Il Giornale d'Italia" stated that there are various issues related to all countries, whose scope extends beyond the territory of Europe. Since the meeting between the Soviet Russian Foreign Minister and the Italian Prime Minister, international relations have been clarified, and these issues related to the overall situation are easier to resolve. In short, the comments made by various newspapers on the talks between the representatives of Italy and Russia are not very clear and are mutually contradictory. Considering this, the representatives of Italy and Russia merely conducted a general discussion of the international political situation, without seeing any specific decisions. It is also unlikely that there will be any changes in the diplomatic policies of the two countries. (4th Havas Dispatch)

Russian Warship Visit to Italy Well-Received, Moscow Sends Telegram of Thanks

Rome - The Soviet fleet traveled to Turkey and detoured to the port of Naples in Italy, where it received a warm welcome from Italy. Soviet Defense Commissioner Voroshilov recently sent a telegram to Prime Minister and Minister of the Navy Mussolini expressing his gratitude, briefly stating, "The commander of our fleet reported that he received gracious hospitality from your country on the way back from Turkey. I am deeply grateful." (4th Dentsu Telegram)

Italy and France Seek Economic Understanding

(Paris) - The Italian-French Economic Understanding Committee held its first meeting today. Chairman and French Member of Parliament Former Cabinet Minister Falgos explained that Italian-French relations have always been amicable, with the same interests. Therefore, it is very important to restore normal trade between the two countries. (4th Havas Dispatch)

Meeting Between American and Russian Ambassadors in Paris

(Paris) - The Chargé d'Affaires of the American Embassy in France, Marinier, and the secretary of the embassy, Duke, went to the Soviet Russian embassy this morning and discussed matters at length with Ambassador Dovgalevsky. This is the first time that the American and Russian embassies in Paris have directly contacted each other since the establishment of the Soviet Russian government. (4th Havas Dispatch)

Litvinov-Mussolini Talks Involve the Far East, Economic Boycott Seals Japan's Fate

Rome - Soviet Russia has signed non-aggression treaties with its Western neighbors and recently restored Russo-American relations. Its diplomatic relations are proceeding smoothly. Now, only the Far Eastern diplomacy with Japan as the opponent has not been resolved. During the first meeting between Litvinov and Mussolini, Li discussed the Far East issue, saying that Soviet Russia must pay attention to Japan's recent continental policy. The two exchanged various opinions on the policy towards Japan. Although Litvinov expressed his opinions on Japanese imperialism, Mussolini only pointed out the issue of Japanese goods entering the world market and did not actively express opinions on Japan. However, newspapers in Rome have recently carried reports of the threat of Japanese goods to the European economy, advocating that all countries unite to boycott Japanese goods. (4th Rengo Telegram)

Famous Italian Reporter Advocates Improving Russian-Italian Business Relations

Rome - Famous Italian reporter Anglai published an article in the newspaper today, advocating that the Russian side automatically reduce the amount of wood transported into Italy, so that Italy can purchase wood from Austria, thereby promoting economic relations between Italy and Austria. In the first eight months of this year, the goods that Italy shipped to Russia were worth 11 million rubles, but the Russian goods imported by Italy were worth 15 million rubles. Therefore, Italy urgently wants to correct the trade deficit. Anglai also believes that the conclusion of a friendship and non-aggression agreement between Italy and Russia may open a new era in European policy, because in this way, countries can be connected with each other through similar bilateral treaties to replace the multilateral agreements of the League of Nations. (4th Reuters Dispatch)

Movement for Small Entente Countries to Recognize Soviet Russia Gains Momentum

Prague - The movement to establish normal diplomatic relations between the Soviet Union and Czechoslovakia is gaining momentum. Several public groups have passed resolutions, and some public officials have delivered speeches, supporting the immediate establishment of normal relations between the Czechs and Soviets. The Economic Committee of the Upper House passed a motion urging the government to conduct negotiations for the restoration of diplomatic relations with the Soviet Union as soon as possible. A few days ago, Minister of Justice Mestan publicly declared his support for the recognition of the Soviet Union. "Demokratis Treat" reported that in the near future, the Small Entente countries will conduct a concerted movement to establish normal diplomatic relations with the Soviet Union. (3rd Vas Telegram)

Small Baltic States Ratify Non-Aggression Treaty with Russia, Russia and Latvia Sign Trade Agreement

(Moscow) - The ambassadors of Estonia and Latvia submitted documents ratifying the London Convention Defining Aggressors to the People's Commissariat for Foreign Affairs today. The documents were signed by the leaders of Estonia and the President of the Republic of Latvia, respectively. Now, prior to this and the above-mentioned ratifications of the two countries, the convention has come into effect between the Soviet Union, Poland, Romania, Persia, Afghanistan, Estonia, and Latvia. Also, according to news received here, the Lithuanian government has also ratified the convention. (4th TASS Telegram)

(Moscow) - A trade agreement between the Soviet Union and the Republic of Latvia was signed here today. The Latvian delegation that negotiated the trade agreement arrived in Moscow a few days ago. The delegation includes Latvian Deputy Minister of Foreign Affairs Mentoss, Governor of the National Bank Turins, and Director of the Industrial Department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Frahmanis. (4th TASS Telegram)

Results of the Spanish Parliamentary Elections - Right Wing Fails to Occupy Absolute Majority - Central Parties Hold Decisive Influence - General Strike Wave Occurs in Coria

Madrid - The results of the Spanish parliamentary elections have now been announced by the government as follows: Right wing 207, Central 167, Left wing 99 (including the Socialist Party). Although the victory of the Madrid Socialist Party has slightly moderated the radicals, the situation in the province of Barcelona is very tense. The governor has ordered the transport strikers to resume work tonight, otherwise they will be dismissed. The national situation is still extremely precarious. The government is concerned about the rebellion of rioters. All newspapers must submit sample copies to the censorship office one hour before publication. News of strikes has been mostly deleted. One newspaper has been seized. It is extremely difficult for radical leader Lerroux to form a cabinet, as Azaña now wants to force the president to dissolve the new parliament, believing that this parliament is not suitable for the current political system. (5th Reuters Dispatch)

Madrid - A revolutionary general strike has been declared in Coria, 200 miles from the capital. Telephone and telegraph lines have been cut off. A large number of police officers are rushing to the area. The Governor of Barcelona's sad letter to the strikers will expire tonight. There are fears of major riots in the area. All passenger and transportation matters in the city are now under the control of the provincial governor. (5th Reuters Dispatch)

Indo-Japanese Conference Again on the Verge of Collapse - Indian Final Reply Has Strong Stance - Japanese Representative Very Embarrassed, Preparing to Return Home

New Delhi - The Indian delegation today sent a detailed reply to the Japanese delegation. The Indo-Japanese negotiations have reached the final stage. It is heard that the Indian government has made some concessions, but maintains a firm stance, stating that if Japan does not accept this method, the negotiations will end without result. The Japanese delegation stated that it now needs to consult Tokyo. However, the Indian government is now preparing for the Japanese government to accept the actions after this final method. (4th Reuters Dispatch)

New Delhi - At the 14th meeting of the Indo-Japanese negotiations, the content of the new proposal put forward by the Indian representative was very different from the final proposal of the Japanese delegation. Japanese Representative Sawada stated that this new proposal leaves no room for consideration by Japan. Representative Sawada telegraphed the Ministry of Foreign Affairs last night for instructions. The Japanese Cotton Industry Delegation believes that the negotiations have reached the point of collapse and is preparing to return home. (4th Rengo Telegram)

Indian Final Answer

Osaka - According to the telegram received by the Textile Federation from the Delhi Delegation at 8:00 PM on the 4th, the content of the answer submitted by the Indian side at the 14th Main Conference between Japan and India on the 4th consists of the following two items: (1) Cotton cloth is divided into four types, and the ratio is revised as follows: Unprocessed cotton cloth 41%, Unprocessed printed cotton cloth 12%, Bleached cotton cloth 12%, Processed cotton cloth 32%. (2) The overall allocation ratio of the four types proposed by Japan is acknowledged as 10% flexible, but this 10% is allocated to more than two types. When the flexibility is in one type, it is 4%. According to this second alternative, all types are still in accordance with the Indian proposal of 45% for unprocessed, 13% for printed, 8% for bleached, and 34% for processed. The flexibility for one type is 4%. As a result, bleached cotton cloth is still the same as the first proposal, at 12%, which is very different from the Japanese final proposal of 18% for bleached cotton cloth. Representative Sawada telegraphed the Textile Federation for instructions. The Textile Federation, the Export Cotton Yarn and Cloth Association, and the Japanese Cotton Association will hold a joint special committee at noon on the 5th to study countermeasures. Private industry operators still insist on adhering to Japan's final proposal. (5th Dentsu Telegram)

Japan Cannot Acknowledge

(Tokyo) - Regarding the Indian response to the Indo-Japanese consultations yesterday, the Foreign Ministry authorities told reporters that they have not yet received an official telegram. If the content of the Indian response is as rumored, then India's sincerity is questionable and unexpected. Once the official telegram is received, the opinions of the parties concerned will be heard. If the response is as rumored, it is too far from Japan's final proposal and cannot be acknowledged. The future of the conference is of great concern. Japan hopes that India will recognize Japan's position and respond with a response that has been given considerable consideration. The result is regrettable. (5th Dentsu Telegram)

New Delhi - The 14th Main Conference of the Indo-Japanese consultations, which received the final response from the Indian side, opened at 11:00 AM on the 4th. Representative Buya gave a comprehensive and detailed response to the maximum concession proposed by Japan. The content of the response only perfunctorily expressed a few concessions and was substantially equivalent to rejecting the Japanese proposal. It is the worst response for Japan and cannot be acknowledged. Representative Sawada believed that it was necessary to seek instructions from the home country and avoided immediate response. The meeting ended in 30 minutes. The situation is increasingly urgent. Japan has decided to support the previous final proposal. There is only a breakdown in the negotiations. In short, the fate of the Indo-Japanese consultations depends on how the Japanese side takes action in the future. (5th Dentsu Telegram)

Osaka - In order to discuss the measures for the response proposed by the Indian side at the 14th Indo-Japanese Main Conference on the 4th, the three groups of the Textile Federation, the Export Cotton Yarn and Cloth Association, and the Cotton Association will hold a joint committee at the Cotton Industry Club at noon today after receiving a detailed report from Representative Kurata. However, the Indian response is very different from Japan's maximum concession proposal, and there is dissatisfaction with everything. The parties concerned have a strong attitude of adhering to Japan's final proposal and rejecting the Indian proposal. Before the meeting of the committee, Textile Federation Chairman Abe Fusajiro told reporters that India's response could not be acknowledged and that Japan's proposal of 18% bleached cotton cloth ratio should be adhered to from beginning to end. (5th Dentsu Telegram)

Hirota Already Concerned About Japan's Economic Aggression - Attaches Importance to the Trend of Various Countries Rejecting Japanese Goods - Instructs Envoys to Mitigate Anti-Japanese Public Opinion

(Tokyo) - According to a telegram received by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini seemed to have discussed the Far East policy with Soviet Russian representative Litvinov who came to Italy, and also discussed the entry and exit of Japanese goods. At the same time, the news in France and Italy is worried about the Japanese goods nibbling on the Ethiopian market, saying that Italy may consider resisting the dumping of Japanese goods. Therefore, the Foreign Ministry authorities attached great importance to the trend of various countries preventing Japanese trade and immediately telegraphed the resident officials, instructing them to mitigate the anti-Japanese public opinion. In addition, Foreign Minister Hirota also reported to the cabinet meeting today and discussed countermeasures. (1st Dentsu Telegram)

Pan-American Conference Discusses Economic Issues; U.S. Yet to Clearly State Position

Although Washington has declared that the U.S. delegation does not want to discuss tariffs or currency stabilization at the Montevideo Pan-American Conference, current indications are that these two issues, along with other important economic matters, will likely become the main topics of the conference. During today's main committee meeting, Mexican Foreign Minister Caso Rangel began a general debate on economic issues, discussing matters such as debt, silver, and currency. Many other representatives also believe that these issues should all be brought up for consideration at the conference. The conference agenda will be decided at tomorrow's main committee meeting, and it is anticipated that the Latin American republics, under the leadership of Caso Rangel, will strongly push for their inclusion. However, whether the United States will actively oppose this remains unclear. Besides the aforementioned declaration from Washington when the U.S. delegation departed, there has been no explicit rejection of discussing tariffs and currency issues. Even the head of the U.S. delegation, Secretary of State Hull, has remained silent on his government's stance. Many other Latin American representatives regard these two issues as vital to their own interests. Latin America has long fiercely criticized U.S. tariff policies. Argentina, in particular, whose beef, leather, and other products have effectively been excluded from the U.S. market, is expected to strongly demand significant modifications to certain U.S. tax rates this time. In today's speech, Caso Rangel emphasized the necessity of reforming commercial relations among the Americas, arguing that such relations should be built on a solid commercial foundation. He stated, "If our several countries wish to have satisfactory commercial relations, they can only be based on genuine mutual benefit. While the development of transportation and bilateral or multilateral agreements are also helpful, what we need most is for the former spiritual friendship or shared history between us to be transformed into genuine economic interests. We live in an era where only by exchanging goods and services with each other can we hope to create an effective economic union." Subsequently, upon a motion by U.S. delegation head Hull, the main committee unanimously elected Uruguayan Foreign Minister Mañé as the permanent chairman of the conference. (National Telegram, 4th)

Montevideo: It is reported that the majority of delegates attending the Pan-American Conference strongly support including silver on the agenda. The Mexican delegation is actively promoting its proposed seven-point monetary and economic plan, in which silver plays a significant role. Mexican Foreign Minister Caso Rangel has disclosed the following details:

(1) All North and South American countries should adopt a bimetallic standard and stabilize the price of silver.

(2) Monetary policy should be based on the domestic price level.

(3) Central banks should be standardized.

(4) An American International Clearing House should be established to reduce unnecessary gold flows.

(5) Silver should be included in central bank reserves.

(6) Currency markets should be controlled.

(7) Credit mediums should be standardized.

Experts here say that if adopted, the Mexican plan could greatly increase the purchasing power of China, India, and other countries holding large quantities of silver, while also consolidating the position of gold standard countries. According to the Mexican Foreign Minister, this proposal is not unique to Mexico; many other representatives are also preparing to add new topics to the economic portion of the agenda. (National Telegram, 4th)

Montevideo: Today, the Cuban delegate issued a statement criticizing other Latin American countries for refusing to recognize the Cuban government of San Martín and appealing for fair treatment of small countries facing the threat of being swallowed by larger ones. (National Telegram, 4th)

Pan-European Economic Conference Forms Permanent Council; Dutch Delegate Expresses Views on Bimetallism

Vienna: Today marked the final day of the Pan-European Economic Conference. A permanent council has been formed. Sir Henri Deterding, Director-General of Royal Dutch Shell, stated in his report on bimetallism that to avoid monetary panic, private individuals should not hold gold; it should only be held by central banks. He endorsed the theories of Gilbart, believing that paper money is superior to silver coins, but he considered hard currency better than Soviet paper money. European central banks should have banknotes backed by silver. He also felt that a unified gold standard was impossible. Deterding did not say that the best thing to do was to close universities that study higher economics, and to instead have more schools that focused on appropriate vocations. (Reuters, 5th)

Tariff Dispute: Anglo-French Negotiations at an Impasse; France Demands Amendment to Commercial Treaty as Condition for Removing Additional Tax

(London): According to various morning newspapers, negotiations between Britain and France regarding the removal of the 15% additional tax levied by France on British goods appear to have reached an impasse again. It is reported that France is demanding an amendment to the Anglo-French Commercial Treaty as a condition for its removal. The French ambassador to Britain has requested the immediate commencement of negotiations for a new agreement. The British cabinet is divided on its approach to the situation, but a tariff war between the two countries is unlikely. (National Telegram, 5th)

Strict Regulations on Opium in Singapore; Government Monopoly on Opium Sales; Smokers Must Register

Singapore: The Straits Settlements government has implemented stricter new regulations concerning the sale of opium paste and the registration of opium smokers in order to purchase opium. As a result, many upper-class Chinese in Singapore have entered Chinese-run opium cessation hospitals in order to quit the habit and avoid humiliation when buying opium. One of the new regulations requires smokers, except those physically unable to leave their homes for special reasons, to purchase opium directly from government outlets. The opium purchase permit includes a photograph of the individual and specifies their daily opium consumption, place of birth, earning capacity, current address, and the location where they intend to smoke the purchased opium. (Reuters, 5th)

Bulk of Narcotics Smuggled into the U.S. Comes from Japan

(Washington): According to the annual report of the Federal Narcotics Commission, the largest quantity of narcotics smuggled into the United States each year consists of morphine originating from Japan. (National Telegram, 4th)

New Papal Representative to China Appointed

Rome: The Pope has recently appointed Archbishop Zanin as the Papal Representative to China, succeeding Archbishop Celso Costantini. Archbishop Zanin currently serves as Secretary-General of the Superior Council of St. Peter's, which handles matters related to indigenous clergy in various countries. (Havas, 4th)

Turkey's Five-Year Plan for Industrial and Commercial Revival; Government Compels Farmers to Wear Standard Clothing to Promote Domestic Goods

Ankara: According to well-informed sources, cabinet members have been meeting for several days, chaired by President Atatürk, specifically to discuss the adoption of a five-year plan for the revival of industry and commerce. (Havas, 5th)

Angora: To encourage the domestic weaving industry, the Turkish government has decided on a standard clothing style for all farmers, male and female, nationwide, which will be enforced. (National Telegram, 4th)

Southern Ireland's Independence Movement; British Government Prepares Response, Declaring Loss of Privileges

(London): Éamon de Valera, President of the Executive Council of the Irish Free State, has requested the British government to clarify its attitude towards Southern Ireland's declaration of a republic. The British cabinet committee has drafted a response, clearly stating that if the Free State secedes from the British Empire, it will naturally forfeit the privileges it enjoys as a member of the Empire. This decision is highly significant, as the committee comprises Prime Minister MacDonald, Dominions Secretary Thomas, Foreign Secretary Simon, and War Secretary Hailsham. The content of the response, to be disclosed in both houses of Parliament tomorrow, essentially states that Britain desires friendly relations with the Free State and has no intention of coercion. (Reuters, 4th)

(London): Dominions Secretary Thomas stated in the House of Commons today regarding the Irish situation that the British government does not believe the Irish Free State will definitively repudiate the Anglo-Irish Treaty, and therefore cannot declare its attitude. (Reuters, 5th)

French Financial Bill; Public Debate in Parliament Tomorrow; Fate of Chautemps Cabinet Hangs in the Balance

(Paris): The Chamber of Deputies' Finance Committee is currently busy amending the government's financial bill. With the exception of a bond lottery in 1934, virtually every clause is being revised. The Socialists' opposition to the reduction of civil servants' salaries is intensifying. Securities market insiders widely believe that the government has little hope of winning the debate in the Chamber of Deputies on Thursday. (Reuters, 4th)

(Paris): After listening to the Budget Minister's explanation of Article 12 of the budget bill (regarding the re-taxation of civil servants' salaries), the rapporteur, Jacques, declared that he believed the clause should be passed in its entirety and requested the committee to vote only on its approval or rejection without amendment. The vote resulted in 19 votes for and 19 votes against, and Jacques' motion was not adopted. Subsequently, the various amendments were put to a vote, and two were rejected. The committee asked the chairman to inform the government that it should thoroughly explain all reasons to the Chamber of Deputies before the public debate. After discussion, the committee passed Article 12 by 19 votes to 17, with two abstentions. (Havas, 4th)

Austria Suppresses National Socialist Party; All Assets Confiscated; Leader Frauenfeld Arrested

Vienna: Based on the declaration issued in June that the National Socialist Party is an illegal organization, Austrian police have now issued a notice that all assets of the National Socialist Party throughout Austria are to be confiscated by the police. (Reuters, 4th)

Vienna: Frauenfeld, the leader of the National Socialist Party branch, was recently arrested by police in the capital. The police department declined to issue a statement on the matter. According to private sources, Frauenfeld will be charged with treason and immediately brought to court for trial. (Havas, 4th)

The United States Lifts Prohibition Starting Today; Nation Prepares for Unrestrained Drinking

(Washington): As the entire United States prepares to celebrate the lifting of Prohibition tomorrow, news suddenly arrived from Utah that the state's National Assembly may not be able to pass the lifting of Prohibition and approve the twenty-first new amendment before 7 PM. Therefore, the nationwide lifting of Prohibition is likely to be delayed until Wednesday. However, hotels, restaurants, bars, and nightclubs all hope that Prohibition will be lifted tomorrow night. Reservations for planned banquets have been fully booked for weeks. At this time, the U.S. President has signed the brewing industry regulations and indicated that import wine tonnage permits will be ready for issuance tomorrow. However, passports can only be issued after the Utah National Assembly officially approves the lifting of Prohibition. The Federal Alcohol Control Administration held meetings all night today, finalizing the number of categories that various countries can import into the United States. (National Telegram, 4th)

Antarctic Scientific Expedition

Dunedin (New Zealand): In the coming months, two expeditions will attempt to uncover the mysteries of the Antarctic continent. The first expedition departed from here this morning by ship, bound for Whale Bay, where it will spend three to four weeks making final preparations before heading to the Southern Ocean. The leader of the expedition is Lieutenant Colonel Ellsworth, and the crew includes Norwegian pilot Bernt Balchen, who previously flew over Antarctica with Byrd. The expedition's goal is to fly completely over the Antarctic continent, taking aerial photographs of the terrain and setting a new record in exploration. It is scheduled to be completed and return by February of next year. The other expedition, led by Rear Admiral Byrd, will arrive here soon and will also head to the Antarctic continent. However, Byrd's expedition will focus on scientific measurements and will remain for two years, differing slightly in nature from Ellsworth's, which emphasizes discovery and exploration. (National Telegram, 5th)

I have come to Nanjing to bid farewell to the authorities of your country and will leave for Shanghai on the evening of the 6th to await passage home by ship. I have spent several years in China and love your country very much. I am truly reluctant to leave China this time under orders." Executive Yuan Interprets Ambiguities in Regulations on Church Land Leases

(Nanjing): The Executive Yuan, upon submission by Lu Bohong, has requested clarification of ambiguities in Articles 1 and 3 of the Provisional Regulations on Land and House Leases by Foreign Churches in the Interior. After review by the Ministry of Interior, the following interpretation is provided: "The Provisional Regulations on Land and House Leases by Foreign Churches in the Interior were originally intended to protect sovereignty and prevent foreigners from purchasing land. If the 'National Catholic Association of China', the responsible party, and the participating believers are indeed citizens of the Republic of China and have been confirmed by the Central or local senior party headquarters as a national religious body, then they are not subject to the restrictions of Articles 1 and 3 of the Provisional Regulations. However, if foreign believers falsely claim Chinese citizenship and purchase land within the association, the local government should strictly crack down to protect sovereignty." The Yuan will distribute this to the Ministries of Finance and Foreign Affairs and order the provincial and municipal governments to take note. (Special Dispatch, 5th)

The Japanese Consul has replied that the matter has been reported to his government and that it has been approved to issue a prohibition order. (Special Dispatch, 5th)

Nanjing Municipal Government Expedites Procedures for Receiving Funds from the Netherlands

(Nanjing): A portion of the Boxer Indemnity returned by the Netherlands is allocated for water conservancy expenses in Nanjing. The municipal authorities, having decided to allocate 100,000 yuan from this indemnity for the partial dredging of the city's sewers, to be received in ten monthly installments of 10,000 yuan each, originally planned to begin receiving the funds from the Dutch side in August of this year. However, due to the fact that the procedures for receiving the funds have not yet been signed, the funds have not been received. The municipal government is now urging the Dutch engineer to come to Nanjing as soon as possible and has sent a letter to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs requesting that the procedures be signed this year so that the funds can be received starting in January next year. The term of the engineer, Mr. Koopmans, is determined to be two years, with a monthly salary of 1,800 yuan. (Special Dispatch, 5th)

Postponement of the National Conscription Law

(Nanjing) The National Conscription System, after the Legislative Yuan formulated the National Conscription Law and forwarded it to the National Government for promulgation, was followed by the Ministries of Military Administration, General Staff, Training, General Staff Headquarters, and Education jointly determining the implementation details. These details were submitted to the Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission for review last month. Originally, it was planned to implement the system in different regions within the year. However, it is heard that Chairman Chiang, considering the post-war recovery in bandit-controlled areas and the need for reorganization, as well as the fact that there are already too many soldiers, finds it difficult to implement the national conscription system immediately. Furthermore, the draft implementation details prepared by the Ministries of Military Administration and General Staff require further detailed consideration. Therefore, it is proposed to postpone the implementation. (5th Dispatch)

Ministry of Finance Newly Sets Tax Rates for Cigarettes, Cement, and Matches

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance has newly set cigarette tax rates: the first grade is taxed at 60 yuan, and the second grade is taxed at 80 yuan. The establishment of cigarette factories is limited to Shanghai, Tianjin, Hankou, and Qingdao. Factories in other places are required to relocate within a time limit. If they fail to do so, the government will assess their value and take them back. Hand-rolled cigarettes are strictly prohibited. Cement is taxed at 1.2 yuan per 170-kilogram barrel. For matches, phosphorus sulfide matches are taxed at 10.08 yuan for Grade A and 13.5 yuan for Grade B. Safety matches are taxed at 13.5 yuan, 17.5 yuan for Grade B, and 25 yuan for Grade C. All are to be implemented starting from the 5th. (5th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Jiangsu to Change Administrative District System

(Zhenjiang) The administrative system of Jiangsu Province has been planned for a long time since Chen Guofu took over the province. According to a certain official of the provincial government, the administrative inspector system of Jiangsu Province will indeed be changed, reducing the number of administrative regions and increasing the powers of the inspectors, to actually supervise county administration. Inspectors will not concurrently serve as county magistrates, and each county may establish an inspector's office. The inspector will examine the administration of each county. In case of an emergency, the inspector may appoint personnel to act as county magistrate. The inspector's offices in each district may also be changed as needed. For example, the first district inspector's office is planned to be set up in Liyang. All measures are still being discussed in the Department of Civil Affairs and can be implemented starting from January 1, 1934. (5th Dispatch)

The Disaster of Two Leaders of the Jilin Volunteer Army: Sun Chaoyang Arrested, Fu Dianchen Killed in Battle

Beiping Correspondence: The Northeast Volunteer Army has been fighting desperately against the Japanese and puppet troops in recent years without support or supplies, and has suffered heavy casualties. Recently, there has been news that two leaders, Sun Chaoyang and Fu Dianchen, have been arrested and killed in battle, respectively. The details of their situations are recorded as follows, in the hope that the people of the country will hear of it and rise up.

Sun Chaoyang

Sun's name is Xingzhou, from Chaoyang County, Rehe Province, about thirty years old. Before the Incident, he was disheartened by national affairs and took his wife and children to do business in Acheng, Jilin. He was clever and his business thrived. After the September 18th Incident, he was saddened by the invasion of the violent Japanese and rose up to raise the banner, gathering thousands of comrades to conduct guerrilla warfare between Harbin and Bin County. He repeatedly defeated the Japanese and puppet military police, and his prestige shook for a time. He also frequently dispatched comrades to form special agent groups, sneaking into Harbin to kidnap the families of puppet officials and wealthy Japanese and Korean residents, and using the funds to supplement military supplies. Together with the volunteer armies of Chen Zongdai, Fu Dianchen, Song Guorong, Mao Zuobin and others, they were regarded as a major threat by the Japanese and puppet authorities, and this time, they deployed 50,000 troops to clear and suppress them in separate areas. Since the start of the attack, the volunteer armies in Jilin have suffered greatly under pressure. Although they have all maintained their unyielding spirit and resisted repeatedly, they have been unable to provide supplies and have limited ammunition. In addition, the high-pressure power of the Japanese Air Force has made it impossible for the various units to communicate and support each other, and casualties have been extremely heavy. Under these circumstances, Sun had no choice but to lead his troops to retreat into the eastern mountains to lie in wait for an opportunity. He himself, accompanied by a staff officer, disguised themselves as farmers and planned to come to Beiping to ask for instructions from a certain national salvation organization. Unfortunately, at about 2:00 AM on October 24, in the seventh carriage of the eleventh small-ticket train from Harbin to Changchun, he was discovered by Guo, a secret agent of the Harbin Mobile Police Team. Because his eyes were bright and his spirit was excellent, he looked like someone who had been in the military for a long time, and not like a farmer. They began to investigate and question him, monitoring his actions. When the train arrived at Guxiangtun Station, Guo led several road police officers to force him off the train and detain him in the Zhanlu police station, and telegraphed the Mobile Police Headquarters. Zhang Shuping, the first section chief of the headquarters, led a squad of police officers in two police cars to Gujiatun Station to escort him back to the headquarters. The headquarters chief, Yu Jinghuan, personally interrogated him strictly. Sun initially falsely claimed to be a farmer from Zhuhe County, but after the team took out a photo for comparison, he generously admitted that he was Sun Chaoyang himself. He planned to go to Beiping to ask a certain national salvation group for instructions. Currently, there are still more than 2,000 people under his command, led by trusted personnel, lying dormant in the eastern mountains. Now, he has been unfortunately arrested, and his ambitions have not been fulfilled. Such is his fate, and he only asks to die quickly. Upon receiving the confession, the team telegraphed the Japanese and puppet military authorities. The captain of the Japanese garrison brigade in Harbin and the captain of the Fu Jiadian gendarmerie were very concerned and wanted to take him to their team for interrogation. After some negotiation, the gendarmerie took him for interrogation. It is reported that Sun's troops have received news of Sun's arrest, and more than 30 loyal members of his troops have formed a suicide squad to enter Harbin to try to rescue Sun and return him to the team. At the same time, they are negotiating with the puppet rewards bureau to exchange Sun for the Japanese kidnapped by Sun's troops earlier. If they do not agree, they will kidnap more important Japanese and Manchurian officials in exchange.

Fu Dianchen

Since raising the banner of righteousness, Fu has led his troops to roam between Yitong, Shuangyang, and Panshi counties in Jilin Province, repeatedly destroying the Jihai railway line, exhausting the Japanese and puppet military police. This time, when the Japanese and puppet troops decided to launch a large-scale attack, Fu led his troops to retreat to the Laoye Ridge area, where they were surrounded by more than 10,000 Japanese and puppet troops. After several days of clashes, they were unable to escape, and the air force bombings caused heavy casualties. He then ordered his troops to surrender temporarily to resolve this crisis. He and three trusted aides left the team to avoid danger temporarily. Unexpectedly, they encountered puppet troops on the road and engaged in a fierce firefight. In the end, due to the disparity in strength, he died on the battlefield. It is truly lamentable.

Zunhua After the War: 70-80% of Shops Closed, An Increasing Number of Vagrants Disturb the People

Zunhua Correspondence: Since the Incident, bandits have been rampant in this county, and robberies have occurred repeatedly in the county seat. The people have become frightened birds. In addition, affected by the war, businesses are sluggish and the market is cold, which has never happened in previous years. According to recent statistics, 70-80% of the shops in the county have closed down. There are few pedestrians on the streets every day, and even fewer shoppers. The poverty of the people and the merchants is evident. Many people are forced to take risks out of desperation, leading to an increase in bandits. Those who are law-abiding freeze and starve to death. In addition, because the county seat is closer to the Great Wall, Japanese and Korean vagrants have been seeking to establish foreign firms due to the geographical location, specializing in selling drugs and guns, and colluding with ruffians to commit illegal acts. The people are adding fuel to the fire and crying out in pain, hoping that the authorities will provide relief. Also, because of the increasing number of bandits, the county authorities announced martial law immediately after the takeover to prevent any eventuality and to secure the area. Recently, in order to further prevent bandits, pedestrians are cut off at 8:00 PM every night. (3rd)

Tight Defense of Chaoshan: Zhang Ruigui Will Serve as Chaoshan Garrison Commander, All Counties Rush to Build Roads, Trenches, and Airfields

Shantou Correspondence: Guangdong Province has drawn troops from Fujian to deploy a tight defense along the border. Chaoshan is close to Fujian Province and is also very important. Therefore, Chen Jitang has again ordered Zhang Ruigui's division to be responsible for the defense of Chao'an, Raoping, and the coastal areas of Chaoshan, and will appoint Zhang as the Chaoshan Garrison Commander or Fortress Commander. The Shantou urban area is still garrisoned by Zhang Wentao's Independent Third Regiment. The guard teams of Jieyang, Puning, and Chaoyang counties will be reorganized into training regiments, with He Baoshu as the commander. The roads in Chaozhou and Meizhou counties are being rushed to be repaired, and all bridges, culverts, and stone work must be completed within 20 days to accommodate large vehicles. Chen Jitang has purchased 30 large vehicles from Hong Kong for military transport. In terms of the air force, Huang Guangrui has dispatched the Second Squadron to Meixian County to cooperate with Wu Wenjian's Fifth Squadron to conduct daily reconnaissance flights on the Fujian-Jiangxi border. Jiaoling, Dapu, Pingyuan, Raoping, and Fengshun all have extremely large defensive works. The Hulu Mountain outside the North Gate of Chao'an City and the Pen Holder Mountain across the river have been selecting construction workers in Shantou for days to rush to build new-style artillery forts and trenches. The trench forts attached to Fengshun County City started construction three months ago and cost more than 200,000 yuan in iron ash. Now, they are rushing to build day and night to complete them within 10 days and are conscripting workers from the people, paying each person 1.5 cents per day. The largest airfield in Xingning County is also rushing to be built, starting on the 23rd, with a circumference of two li, and the location surrounds the middle of the Diaofang Dam, which can accommodate hundreds of aircraft for takeoff and landing. Li Yangjing, the commander of the Third Army, inspected the East River on the 26th, passing through Huizhou, Zijin, and Wuhua to Meixian, presiding over military affairs. It is heard that Li will be in the upper reaches of the Han River between Zijin and Fengshun, coordinating military operations against Fujian and temporarily adopting a strict defensive posture. (November 27)

Hankou Citizens' Assembly - Passing a Resolution to Condemn the Chen-Li Case -

Hankou Correspondence: The Hankou citizens' assembly was held at 9:00 AM on the 4th in the New Market to discuss and condemn the rebellion. More than 20,000 people attended. Before the meeting, leaflets were distributed, and after the meeting, a motorcade paraded through the city. The atmosphere was very tense. The assembly elected Wu Shaoshu as the general chairman, and Chen Guangzu and Wu Guozhen gave speeches. Seven motions were passed on the spot: (1) Telegraphing the Central Government, requesting the National Government to issue a clear order to condemn the rebellion in order to curb chaos and stabilize the Party and the country. (2) Telegraphing the whole country to unanimously urge the government to declare the rebellion. (3) Warning the 19th Route Army to automatically return to the right path and eliminate the puppet organization, otherwise they will cut themselves off from the Party and the country, and be abandoned by the people. (4) Telegraphing the Central National Government to strictly order the authorities in each province and city to prevent the activities of reactionary elements. (5) Telegraphing the Central Executive Committee members in various places to enter Beijing as soon as possible and jointly discuss the elimination of the Min rebels. (6) Telegraphing the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in the name of the assembly to declare the truth about the rebellion in Min Province to various countries and deny all its external relations. (7) Telegraphing the generals and soldiers of the whole country, for the handling of the Min Incident, should adhere to the Central Government's intention and work for the Party and the country. The text of the assembly's telegram to the Central Committee of the Kuomintang is recorded as follows: "This time, Chen Mingshu, Li Jishen, and others seized the border areas, colluded with bandits and served as enemies, changed the era name, rebelled against the Party and harmed the country. Their rebellious actions are obvious. All the people of the country deeply hate them. In recent years, the Communist bandits have been rampant, the red flames have been rampant, the villages have been in ruins, the fields have been covered with thorns, the people's livelihood has been devastated, and foreign aggression has occurred repeatedly. Fortunately, Chairman Chiang, with his mandate in the central hub, has made remarkable achievements in the prompt encirclement. The recent military campaign to suppress bandits in Jiangxi and the various routes in the northwest have made significant progress. The rebels have taken the opportunity to create chaos, colluded with bandits, opened one side of the encirclement net, and undermined the encirclement plan that was about to succeed. The crimes of Chen and Li are too numerous to mention. We hope that the Central Committee will make a grand plan and order the National Government to launch a crusade immediately and eliminate them on a set day. The 800,000 people of Hankou will unite and rise up to pledge their support. We respectfully report this by telegram, hoping you will take it into consideration." The telegram to the 19th Route Army reads: "The country is unfortunate, and disasters are frequent. In recent years, the Red bandits have been rampant, and the people have no food. Foreign enemies are rampant, and the rivers and mountains have changed color. At this time of impending doom, the people have long been tired of chaos. However, Chen Mingshu and others have disregarded the great wrong, advocated chaos in Minyuan, allied with bandits, betrayed the Party, established an organization, and changed the era name, committing heinous crimes that are resented by gods and humans. The generals and soldiers have blindly followed and acted blindly, abandoning a glorious history and leaving behind a curse for ten thousand years. There is no greater folly than the folly of man. The citizens of this city, indignant at the perverse actions of Chen Mingshu and others, held a citizens' assembly to condemn the rebellion today to show their common hatred. We hope that you will awaken and repent, arrest the leading criminals and offer them to the Central Government, and disband the puppet organization in order to set things right. Otherwise, you will harm yourself and the country. The 800,000 people of Hankou will perish together with you. This is telegraphed to you, hoping you will understand." (4th)

Songjiang Extortion Criminal Implicates Teahouse Worker

Someone surnamed in the Hengshan area has some savings and can live without worry. Earlier this month, they suddenly received a threatening letter in the name of the Communist Party. The letter was full of threats, demanding a huge sum of more than 1,000 yuan, and stipulated that the money should be prepared on the 3rd of this month and handed over to someone who would come to collect it from the boat that travels from Hengshan to Song. When the boat arrives, someone will come to collect it. Someone secretly reported this to the County Public Security Bureau. Director Shen immediately sent two secret agents disguised as a monk and a temple servant to Hengshan. They took the boat back to Song on the appointed date. The person surnamed prepared a bundle of paper that looked like banknotes. The name of the recipient was marked on the outside. That morning, a traveler came to the Xiesheng Hotel to stay. He sent the teahouse worker Xu Shunlin to the Hengshan dock to ask the boatman if there was a letter for someone (the name specified in the letter). The boatman gave the teahouse worker the fake letter entrusted by the person surnamed. Just as he was about to put it away, the secret agents disguised as monks jumped out of the boat and arrested Xu and took him to the Xiesheng Hotel. However, the traveler who had come earlier had heard the news and fled. The teahouse worker was taken to the bureau for questioning, and the escaped criminal was ordered to be arrested in order to investigate the matter thoroughly.

A Criminal Who Obstructed Freedom is Arrested

Lu Sheng's daughter, Shu Bao, of the 19th District of Tinglin, married Jiang Shugen. Since their marriage, she has been abused in every way. Her mother, Sheng, came to Songjiang and filed a complaint with the court. Yesterday, the court sent police chief Chen Zhong to the countryside to deliver the summons, including to Lu Shu Bao. Lu Shu Bao shouted for help. Police chief Chen entered the house to investigate and saw that Shu Bao's right foot was chained to a huge rock by her husband, preventing her from moving. Later, the villagers found Liang Shugen and brought him back. He found a way to remove the iron chain and sent the man and woman and Sheng to Songjiang together. The prosecutor Shengku questioned them and ordered Liang Shugen to be detained for obstructing freedom. Lu Shu Bao was taken back by her mother, Sheng, to await summons.

Suzhou Xujiang People Petition for Protection

Xujiang in Suzhou borders Taihu Lake and is located in a dangerous area, which has always been an area where bandits appear. There used to be water police stationed there. Since the water police were reorganized, the local defense has been empty, and the local people are extremely panicked. Yesterday (5th) morning, more than 100 villagers went to the Second District Office in Mudu to petition, demanding that a battalion be sent to garrison as soon as possible to maintain law and order. The district chief Hui Hong urgently telegraphed the Second District of the Water Public Security Bureau, requesting the dispatch of a team to garrison. District Chief Wei, according to the telegram, sent Captain Wang Rongxian of the Fifth Team, leading four gunboats, to garrison in Xujiang.

Public Security Personnel Punished for a Robbery Case in the City

In the robbery case at No. 3 Guangjie, Song Xianzhou Lane in the city, the Public Security Bureau arrested five suspects, Tang Kangqi, Zhu Xiangsheng, Zhang Riyin, etc., and sent them to the court. After investigation by the prosecutor's office, Tang Kangqi, Zhu Xiangsheng, and Zhang Riyin were not prosecuted, and Hu Chuanshou and Zhao Shuqun were given other punishments. The director of the Public Security Bureau, Shen Weiying, was ordered by the province to admonish the director of the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau, Xu Jingqing, and the patrol officer Huang Zuzeng, each with a demerit, and ordered them to arrest the real criminals within five days.

Wuxi Revenge Murder

Deng Zhenquan, a resident of Huangshi Street, 61st District, 15th District (Qingcheng City) in the county, was a tailor by profession and came from a poor family. At about 9:00 PM on the previous night (4th), A Lin, the son of Hong Pei from Zhuangjia Lane, 62nd District, nearby, was drinking with Zhenquan in a certain hotel on the street. Later, because Zhenquan drank too much wine, the two sides had an argument for some reason, which led to violence. Zhenquan, in a moment of anger, punched A Lin twice, but unfortunately hit a vital point, and A Lin fell to the ground and died. Afterwards, someone reported this to Hong Pei, who tied up the murderer Deng Zhenquan with a rope and decided to send him to the city today. The chief of the township also reported the matter to the court for an autopsy. However, it is said that there was another reason why Deng Zhenquan killed A Lin, which led to the tragedy. Also, Wang Yunquan, a villager from Fanjia Bang, Tang Zhuang Township, 355th District, 12th District, was drinking near the Daqiang Gate and returned home the previous night. He met two villagers on the way who were old enemies and beat Xuequan to death. The murderer saw that he had caused a disaster and fled. Later, the chief of the township, Lu Zhongying, came to the city to report the matter to the court and requested an autopsy. According to the report, the prosecutor's office sent the prosecutor and his staff by car to the countryside to conduct an autopsy yesterday (5th). The autopsy revealed that the deceased, Wu Yunquan, died from being beaten. After the autopsy, he ordered the corpse to be placed in a coffin for burial, pending the arrest of the murderer.

Changshu Boat Traveling at Night Encountered Robbery and Capsized

Wang Yongzhang, a musician from Wuxi, came to Changshu with five or six partners the day before yesterday at the invitation of someone surnamed in this county. On the 3rd, they took a boat back to Wuxi. When sailing through Shigubridge in Taihe Township, 9th District of this county, it was already 9:00 PM. Suddenly, they saw many boats, carrying more than a dozen bandits, chasing after them. They realized that something was wrong and urged the boatman to row quickly. Before long, they were overtaken, and they were ordered to stop the boat. Five or six people jumped out and violently attacked the bow of the boat with weapons, and then looted at will. At that time, Wang and others were extremely frightened and tried to avoid being caught, which caused the weight to be uneven and the boat capsized. The bandits and the musicians all drowned at the bottom of the river. When the bandit boat saw what had happened, they quickly rescued their comrades and fled. The musicians were mostly skilled swimmers and did not drown, but the boatman's three-year-old child was not rescued in time and drowned.

Changzhou Zhixin Steamer Crew Beating Person to Death

The Changzhai-bound Zhixin steamer, which runs between Wuyi and Zhaiqiao, departed from Changzhou to Zhaiqiao on the 3rd. While passing through Fangdi, it was already evening. A Zhaiqiao resident named Zhang Jinrong boarded the ship to return home. A quarrel arose with the ship owner, Gu Pandai, and his brother, Rongjin, over ticket purchase, leading to a scuffle. Rongjin happened to be holding a machine steel plate clamp, which he used to injure Zhang Jinrong's waist. Striking a vital point, Zhang suddenly died on the 4th. His wife, Zhang Yangshi, believing her husband's death to be unnatural, immediately reported it to the local Public Security Police Station. The Gu Pandai and Rongjin brothers were placed under supervision, and the report was forwarded to the Nabenzhen District Office for referral to the county court to send personnel to investigate and handle the matter.

Rugao Newlywed Husband Suddenly Arrested

A Yangzhou man named Tang Yaodong, who rented a residence in the Yuanjiaqiao Guanfeng Lane in this county, appeared extravagant. This autumn, he was introduced to and engaged a Chen woman from outside the East Gate. The woman was only eighteen years old. He had just married her the night before. The newlyweds were in blissful harmony when, unexpectedly, around 7 PM last night, several military police arrived and took Tang away. It is said that Tang had committed major theft cases in Hai'an and other places and had been wanted. He has now been sent to Taixian for investigation and handling.

Young Girl Opposes Marriage and Commits Suicide

In Dawangzhuang, Chemahu District, there lived a man named Yu Xi who did not engage in proper work. In the 18th year of the Republic, he joined the Communist Party and engaged in robbery. In the 19th year, he surrendered to the local District Office. Fourteen years ago, he engaged a matchmaker named Liu Gui and betrothed himself to the daughter of Wang Si from Fanjiazhuang. At that time, Wang's daughter was only seven years old, and it was entirely arranged by her parents. Recently, the girl had grown up, gained some knowledge, and learned that Yu, although having surrendered, was still of bad character. She expressed her opposition to her parents and requested the dissolution of the engagement. However, Yu learned of this and secretly bribed the matchmaker, Liu Gui, to facilitate the marriage. After receiving the bribe, Liu Gui went to the Wang family and used all kinds of threats to force Wang to agree. Wang was helpless and had already chosen a date for the wedding. When the girl heard about this, overwhelmed with hatred, she suddenly conceived a suicidal thought. Yesterday, taking advantage of the family's unpreparedness, she hanged herself. It is truly tragic.

Nantong County Public Security Bureau Chief Replaced

Chen Yizhong, the Chief of the Nantong County Public Security Bureau, resigned upon being summoned by Gu Zhutong to Jiangxi to assist in bandit suppression. The province has already appointed Fu Qianzhi to succeed him. Fu will arrive in Nantong within days to take over.

Hangzhou Hushu Fire Causes 100,000 Loss

The Yongcheng Cotton Shop, located on Jiangzhang Bridge, Zhijie Street, Hushu, Hangzhou, owned by Ni Yongcheng from Shaoxing, has been in operation for some time and has a good business. The shop had a large inventory. Yesterday (the 4th) at around 11 PM, the night shift workers stopped work, and the workers went upstairs to sleep. In a daze, they knocked over a kerosene lamp, which fell into the cotton and spread to the wooden walls. In an instant, flames soared. The police on duty at the post heard the alarm and reported it to the headquarters, which alerted the Public Security Bureau's fire brigade and various rescue teams. They rushed to extinguish the fire, which took three hours to put out. It is estimated that 64 shops and houses were burned down, with losses estimated at over 100,000 yuan. The arsonist has been handed over to the Public Security Bureau for transfer to the court for interrogation.

Security Office Executes Four Bandits

The Zhejiang Provincial Security Office, based on the submission from the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau's Military Police Investigation Team, presented five bandits from Sheng County, including Liu Youcai, also known as Lou Houshui, Chen Jincai, Xu Rongsheng, Liu Ayan, and Zhang Jindi. They also presented a female criminal, Zhang Aixian, also known as Yu Zhangshi, who was captured by the Sheng County government. After interrogation, Xu Rongsheng confessed that in April of this month, he and Chen Jincai, Liu Youcai, and six others kidnapped Qian Jingquan from Maojiawan and extorted money. Chen Jincai confessed to being present at the scene. Liu Youcai, Liu Ayan, and others confessed to repeated kidnappings and extortion, as well as opening fire on the base team, killing team member Tong Linhuo. As Xu Rongsheng, Chen Jincai, Liu Youcai, and Liu Ayan were found to have committed unforgivable crimes, they were sentenced to death. Yesterday (the 5th) at 9 AM, the four criminals, including Xu, were taken out, their identities were confirmed, and they were escorted to Qingbo Gate for execution by firing squad.

Ningbo Dongmenkou Fire

The Wanxiang Guiyuan Shop at No. 43 Yuelai Lane, Fangjing Street, Dongmenkou, Ningbo, suddenly caught fire yesterday (the 2nd) at 9 AM. The fire was very fierce and unapproachable. After various water dragons rushed to the scene to put out the fire, it was extinguished after an hour. It is estimated that more than ten houses of three companies including Wanxiang Guiyuan Shop, Yixing Jianhuo Shop, and Gansheng Flower Shop were burned, with losses of more than 40,000 yuan.
